Dear colleagues,

For the project ANR-ALIENTO  we need to recruiter two post-docs for 6 months in order to tag proverb-books or sapiential opera (from Spain) in 1) medieval Hebrew, 2) medieval arabic. Here in attachment you can find the requirements and details.
Informations about ALIENTO can be found in our website www.aliento.eu<http://www.aliento.eu/>
Could you please put the announcement on line in the relevant websites or diffusion-lists you may know, and tell us if you have somebody to recommend.
We hope to hear from you soon,
With our best regards

Prof. Marie-Christine Bornes Varol
Dpt. Etudes Hébraïques & Juives
